339. [Integrate] Random integrate trig 1355: sin2cos2 [format fuzz] [integrate_trig:sin2cos2]
================================================================================
Input:
1
sin(3* x+(pi/3))^2*cos(3*x+  (pi/3))^2
3

Check:
check; calculated answer correctness; random input formatting fuzzed

Output:
1 int | 2 de | 3 param area | M: f: 1 auto | 2 dir | 3 trig | 4 sub | 5 pts | 6 pf | 7 div | Met: Method: Integration by substitution
1. u = 3*x + 1/3*pi
2. du/dx = 3
3. du = 3 dx
4. I = Int[1/3*sin(u)^2*cos(u)^2] du
5. = -1/32*sin(4*u) + 1/8*u + C
6. Substitute back u = 3*x + 1/3*pi.
7. = -1/32*sin(4*(3*x + 1/3*pi)) + 1/8*(3*x + 1/3*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(12*x + 4/3*pi) + 3/8*x + 1/24*pi + C

6. Substitute back u = 2*x - 1/3*pi.
7. = -1/32*sin(4*(2*x - 1/3*pi)) + 1/8*(2*x - 1/3*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(8*x - 4/3*pi) + 1/4*x - 1/24*pi + C

================================================================================
365. [Integrate] Random integrate trig 1328: sin2cos2 [format fuzz] [integrate_trig:sin2cos2]
================================================================================
Input:
1
(sin(6*x +(  - pi  /6))^2*cos(6*  x  +  ( -pi/  6)) **2)
3

check; calculated answer correctness; random input formatting fuzzed

Output:
1 int | 2 de | 3 param area | M: f: 1 auto | 2 dir | 3 trig | 4 sub | 5 pts | 6 pf | 7 div | Met: Method: Integration by substitution
1. u = 6*x - 1/6*pi
2. du/dx = 6
3. du = 6 dx
4. I = Int[1/6*sin(u)^2*cos(u)^2] du
5. = -1/32*sin(4*u) + 1/8*u + C
6. Substitute back u = 6*x - 1/6*pi.
7. = -1/32*sin(4*(6*x - 1/6*pi)) + 1/8*(6*x - 1/6*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(24*x - 2/3*pi) + 3/4*x - 1/48*pi + C
